 There are many farmers in Modinagar area whose crops have been spoiled and who are being forced into the trap of local moneylenders to pay the bank loan
 iske liye wo kaaphi zyaada byaaj par karz uthaa rahe hai
 Sugarcane farmer Sonu of Khanjarpur village in Modinagar had sown sugarcane at a cost of Rs 2 lakh in 20 bighas this year
 sari upaj modinagar ke ek sthaneey chini mil ko de aae lekin 5 lakh kaa bakaayaa abhitak nahin mila
 Sonu had sown wheat right next to his sugarcane which became more difficult due to unseasonal rains
 sonu ne enditivi se kaha, '5 bighas kii fasal barbaad ho gayi he
 Now more grains will not come out of it, there is no payment of sugarcane, there is loss of wheat
 ' In fact, the worst effect of heavy rains has been on those sugarcane farmers who had sown wheat crop along with sugarcane this year
 chini milon ne ganne kaa paisa nahin diya or jo gehun kii fasal thi wo buree tarah kharaab ho chuki he
 Now the pressure on these farmers to repay the loan is also increasing
 sonu par 2

 There was a time, when you had to wish your friends or relatives for a birthday or wedding anniversary, or send a message of happiness and sorrow, you had to depend only on the postman
 
 
 15 paise kaa postcard yaa nile rang kaa antardeshiy patr likhaa jaataa tha, or daalaa jaataa tha, gali-gali main lage hue dak vibhaag ke laal rang ke dibbon main, jinhen letterbox kaha jaataa tha
 
 
 The same thing happened till a few decades ago, but now that box has become a thing of the past
 
 
 telegram, yani taar, bhejnaa bhi gujarey jamaane kii baat ho gai he, or gharon main lage hue landline phone ko bhi log bhuulane lage hai, kyonki zamana ab mobile ho chukaa he
 
 
 Just press some button on your mobile phone and your message will reach in the blink of an eye
 
 
 lekin kya aap jaanate hai, is mobile jamaane ko aae bhi aaj do dashak puure ho gaye hai
 
 
 Actually, the short messaging service, which is sent from mobile, SMS, started 20 years ago, on December 3, 1992, in the UK, on 3 December 1992, an engineer in the UK sent messages from his computer to the mobile via Vodafone network, which Was 'mary Christmas'
 
 
 haalanki esemes bhejne kaa khyaal sabase pehle varsh 1984 main finland ke purv naukarshah mati macconen ke man main aayaa tha, lekin kamyaabi mili british ejeeniyar ko
 
 
 The comments haalanki aaj apni umr ke 21wein paaydaan par pahunchane vaale esemes ko fasebuk or twitor jaisi soshal netwarking websiton se kadi chunauti mil rahi he, lekin aaj bhi puri duniya main chaar arab se zyaada log rozaana mobile ke jariye esemes bhejte hai
 
 
 The SMS also made radical changes in the spelling and alphabet of the prevailing language in view of the need to say at least as many letters as possible, and continued to use only 160 signs to complete the talk, to express laughter and sorrow
 Emoticons were introduced in SMS to show instead of
 
 
 haalanki soshal netwarking websiton ke chalate apane janm se lekar ab tak pyaar, khushi, dukh or nafrat kaa izhaar karne vaale esemes ke istemaal karne vaale logon ke bich pichhali do timahiyon main ek arab kii kami ai he, lekin ummid barkaraar he ki nae-nae prayogon se yah 'chotu miseging' lambe vakt tak apane chaahane waalon ke bich bani rahegi
 
 
 Happy Birthday SMS
 
 
 darasal, mobile se bheje jane vaale short miseging sarvice, yani esemes kii shuruyaat aaj se thik 20 saal pehle varsh 1992 main 3 disambar ko hi britain main ek ejeeniyar dwaara apane computer se vodaphone network ke jariye mobile par sandesh bheje jane se hui thi, jo tha, 'mairi christmas'
 
 
 Although the idea of sending SMS first came to mind in 1984 in the mind of former Finland bureaucrat Matty mcconen, but the British engineer succeeded
 
 
 tippaniyan Although SMS, which reached the 21st position of its age today, is facing a tough challenge from social networking websites like Facebook and Twitter, but even today, more than four billion people across the world send SMS daily via mobile
 
 
 kam se kam aksharon main zyaada se zyaada kah dene kii zarurat ke maddenzar esemes ne prachlit bhashaa kii vartanee or varnmaala main bhi krantikari parivartan kiye, or maatr 160 chihnon main apni baat puri karne ke liye prayog hote rahe, jinke tahat hansi or dukh ko bataane ke bajaae dikhaane ke liye esemes main imoticons laae gaye

 Rani Mukherjee is returning from the big screen with her film Hichki

 The reason for this change is also revealed
 # Hichkishifted ahead
 
 
 Will release on 23 March 2018
 
 
 Reason: Having evoked positive reactions during the private screenings, the marketing / distribution team of YRF convinced Aditya Chopra that the movie should release post exams
 
 
 Hence 23 March 2018
 
 
 Stars Rani Mukerji
 - taran adarsh (@taran_adarsh) February 1, 2018 Trade analyst Taran Adarsh tweeted, Rani Mukherjee's film Hichki will now be released after 23 March 2018
 film kii nijee scruning ke baad mili sakaaratmak pratikriyaayein ko dekhte hue yashraj kii marketing / vitaran team ne aditya chopra ko salaah di he ki film ko pariksha ke baad relies kiya janaa thik rahegaa

 is vajah se use lagaataar hitchkee aati he, jo uske kariyar ke liye ek rukaawat banati he

 But both countries can also try to find a way to reduce dependence on the dollar and make some arrangement for trading in rupee-ruble (russia's currency)

 supreme court ne kendriya shikshan sansthaaon main dharm ke aadhaar par alpsankhyakon ko aarakshan dene kaa nirnay nirast karne ke andhra pradesh hoicourt ke aadesh par roak lagane se inkaar kar diya
 Following this stand of the Supreme Court, 4 for minorities in reputed central educational institutions like Indian Institute of Technology (IIT)
 5 fisadi aarakshan vyavastha ke tahat pravesh kii ummid rakhane vaale 325 chaatro ko maayusi haath lagi he
 After hearing the arguments of Additional Solicitor General Gaurav Banerjee, the vacation bench of Justice KS Radhakrishnan and Justice JS Khehar said in two words, "we will not stay the High Court order
" nyaayadhishon ne sarkaar se sawaal kiya ki anya pichde virgon ke aarakshan main se kya dharm ke aadhaar par is tarah kaa vargeekaran kiya ja saktaa he? The judges also issued notices on the petition of the Ministry of Human Resource Development to R
 Krishnamaiya and the other defendants, on whose petition 4 out of 27% quota of the other backward classes was for the minorities
 5 fisadi aarakshan kaa praavdhaan hoicourt ne nirast kiya tha
 As soon as the case started hearing, the judges said that the Central Government has presented a large number of documents to them in favor of reservation for minorities
 ye dastavej hoicourt main pesh karnaa adhik tarksangat hota
 Additional Solicitor General Gaurav Banerjee said that the High Court felt that this reservation was probably for all minorities
 is par nyaayadhishon ne kaha, aarakshan ke bare main karyaalay ke gyaapan se aisa hi abhas hota he
 Banerjee said that Buddhist and Parsi communities such as Minorities 4
 5 fisadi aarakshan kii suchi main shaamil nahin hai
 He said that religious minority communities are within the purview of 27 per cent reservation for other backward classes, while 4
 5 fisadi ke is hisse ke aarakshan main muslim samaaj ke sabase nichle tabake yaa dharm parivartan karne vaale isaayiyon ko shaamil kiya gaya he
 The judges said that 4
 5 fisadi aarakshan ke bare main 22 disambar, 2011 ko jari karyaalay gyaapan ko koi vidhaayi samarthan bhi praapt nahin tha
 4 out of 27 per cent reservation for other backward classes
 5 fisadi aarakshan kii gananaa par sawaal uthaate hue nyaayadhishon ne jaananaa chaha ki kya is aarakshan ko kisi sanvidhanik yaa vidhaayi sanstha kaa samarthan praapt he? nyaayadhishon ne yah bhi jaananaa chaha ki kya 4
 Does the office memorandum on 5 per cent reservation have any constitutional or legislative support? gaurav banerjee in sawaalon kaa koi santoshjanak jawaab nahin de sake
 He repeatedly requested the judges that the High Court order should be stayed in view of the counseling for admission to the iits, because 4
 5 fisadi aarakshan cote ke tahat hi is varg ke 325 chaatro kii suchi taiyaar kii gai he
 But the judges were not impressed by these pleas and said that they give minorities 4 out of 27 per cent reservation for other backward classes
 5 fisadi aarakshan dene ke nirnay ko nirast karne ke faisle par roak nahin lagaaange
 The comments ucch nyaayalay ne 28 may ko alpsankhyakon ke liye aarakshan kaa praavdhaan asanvaidhanik qaraar de diya tha
 It was only after this that the Ministry of Human Resource Development approached the Supreme Court
 ucchtam nyaayalay ne 11 june ko maanav sansaadhan vikaas mantralay se 4
 All facts and documents related to 5 percent reservation were sought
 nyaayalay ne us din bhi spasht kar diya tha ki sarkaar ko itane jatil or samvedansheel masale ko is tarah se nahin lenaa chahie tha
 Not only this, the apex court had also expressed displeasure over the central government's attitude of blaming the High Court for this odd situation
 nyaayalay kaa kahana tha ki vaastaviktaa to yah he ki centre sarkaar hi is maamle main aavashyak dastavej pesh karne main vifal rahi thi
